#include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <array>
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <random>
#include <execution>
#include <iomanip>

using namespace std;

struct Vector3 {
    double x, y, z;
    Vector3() : x(0), y(0), z(0) {}
    Vector3(double x, double y, double z) : x(x), y(y), z(z) {}
    Vector3 operator+(const Vector3& o) const { return {x+o.x, y+o.y, z+o.z}; }
    Vector3 operator-(const Vector3& o) const { return {x-o.x, y-o.y, z-o.z}; }
    Vector3 operator*(double s) const { return {x*s, y*s, z*s}; }
    double& operator[](int i) { return i == 0 ? x : (i == 1 ? y : z); }
    const double& operator[](int i) const { return i == 0 ? x : (i == 1 ? y : z); }
};

double dot(const Vector3& a, const Vector3& b) { return a.x*b.x + a.y*b.y + a.z*b.z; }
Vector3 cross(const Vector3& a, const Vector3& b) {
    return {a.y*b.z - a.z*b.y, a.z*b.x - a.x*b.z, a.x*b.y - a.y*b.x};
}
double length_squared(const Vector3& a) { return dot(a, a); }
double length(const Vector3& a) { return sqrt(length_squared(a)); }
Vector3 normalize(const Vector3& a) {
    double l = length(a);
    if (l < 1e-12) return {0,0,0};
    return a * (1.0 / l);
}

struct AABB {
    Vector3 min, max;
    AABB() { min = Vector3(1e30, 1e30, 1e30); max = Vector3(-1e30, -1e30, -1e30); }
    void expand(const Vector3& p) {
        min.x = std::min(min.x, p.x); min.y = std::min(min.y, p.y); min.z = std::min(min.z, p.z);
        max.x = std::max(max.x, p.x); max.y = std::max(max.y, p.y); max.z = std::max(max.z, p.z);
    }
    void expand(const AABB& b) {
        expand(b.min); expand(b.max);
    }
    bool overlaps(const AABB& b) const {
        if (max.x < b.min.x || min.x > b.max.x) return false;
        if (max.y < b.min.y || min.y > b.max.y) return false;
        if (max.z < b.min.z || min.z > b.max.z) return false;
        return true;
    }
};

struct BVHNode {
    AABB box;
    int left = -1;
    int right = -1;
    int tri_start = 0;
    int tri_count = 0;
};

struct Mesh {
    std::vector<Vector3> verts;
    std::vector<std::array<int, 3>> faces;
    std::vector<BVHNode> bvh_nodes;
    std::vector<int> bvh_tri_indices;
    std::vector<Vector3> normals;
    
    int build_bvh(int start, int end) {
        int node_idx = bvh_nodes.size();
        bvh_nodes.push_back(BVHNode());
        
        AABB box;
        for (int i = start; i < end; ++i) {
            int t = bvh_tri_indices[i];
            box.expand(verts[faces[t][0]]);
            box.expand(verts[faces[t][1]]);
            box.expand(verts[faces[t][2]]);
        }
        bvh_nodes[node_idx].box = box;
        
        if (end - start <= 4) {
            bvh_nodes[node_idx].tri_start = start;
            bvh_nodes[node_idx].tri_count = end - start;
            return node_idx;
        }
        
        Vector3 extent = box.max - box.min;
        int axis = 0;
        if (extent.y > extent.x && extent.y > extent.z) axis = 1;
        if (extent.z > extent.x && extent.z > extent.y) axis = 2;
        
        double split = (box.min[axis] + box.max[axis]) * 0.5;
        
        int mid = start;
        for (int i = start; i < end; ++i) {
            int t = bvh_tri_indices[i];
            Vector3 centroid = (verts[faces[t][0]] + verts[faces[t][1]] + verts[faces[t][2]]) * (1.0 / 3.0);
            if (centroid[axis] < split) {
                std::swap(bvh_tri_indices[i], bvh_tri_indices[mid]);
                mid++;
            }
        }
        
        if (mid == start || mid == end) {
            mid = start + (end - start) / 2;
        }
        
        int left_child = build_bvh(start, mid);
        int right_child = build_bvh(mid, end);
        bvh_nodes[node_idx].left = left_child;
        bvh_nodes[node_idx].right = right_child;
        
        return node_idx;
    }

    void build() {
        normals.resize(faces.size());
        bvh_tri_indices.resize(faces.size());
        for (size_t i = 0; i < faces.size(); ++i) {
            bvh_tri_indices[i] = i;
            Vector3 v0 = verts[faces[i][0]];
            Vector3 v1 = verts[faces[i][1]];
            Vector3 v2 = verts[faces[i][2]];
            normals[i] = normalize(cross(v1 - v0, v2 - v0));
        }
        if (!faces.empty()) {
            build_bvh(0, faces.size());
        }
    }
};

bool ray_intersects_tri(const Vector3& ro, const Vector3& rd, const Vector3& v0, const Vector3& v1, const Vector3& v2, double& t, double& u, double& v) {
    Vector3 edge1 = v1 - v0;
    Vector3 edge2 = v2 - v0;
    Vector3 h = cross(rd, edge2);
    double a = dot(edge1, h);
    if (a > -1e-9 && a < 1e-9) return false;
    double f = 1.0 / a;
    Vector3 s = ro - v0;
    u = f * dot(s, h);
    if (u < 0.0 || u > 1.0) return false;
    Vector3 q = cross(s, edge1);
    v = f * dot(rd, q);
    if (v < 0.0 || u + v > 1.0) return false;
    t = f * dot(edge2, q);
    if (t > 1e-9) return true;
    return false;
}

bool is_inside(const Mesh& mesh, const Vector3& p) {
    if (mesh.bvh_nodes.empty()) return false;
    std::mt19937 rng(1337);
    std::uniform_real_distribution<double> dist(-1.0, 1.0);
    
    for (int attempts = 0; attempts < 10; ++attempts) {
        Vector3 rd = normalize(Vector3(dist(rng), dist(rng), dist(rng)));
        double min_t = 1e30;
        int hit_tri = -1;
        bool edge_hit = false;
        
        std::vector<int> stack;
        stack.push_back(0);
        while (!stack.empty()) {
            int node_idx = stack.back();
            stack.pop_back();
            const BVHNode& node = mesh.bvh_nodes[node_idx];
            
            double tmin = -1e30, tmax = 1e30;
            for (int i = 0; i < 3; ++i) {
                if (std::abs(rd[i]) < 1e-9) {
                    if (p[i] < node.box.min[i] || p[i] > node.box.max[i]) { tmax = -1e30; break; }
                } else {
                    double ood = 1.0 / rd[i];
                    double t1 = (node.box.min[i] - p[i]) * ood;
                    double t2 = (node.box.max[i] - p[i]) * ood;
                    if (t1 > t2) std::swap(t1, t2);
                    tmin = std::max(tmin, t1);
                    tmax = std::min(tmax, t2);
                }
            }
            if (tmin > tmax || tmin > min_t) continue;
            
            if (node.left == -1) {
                for (int i = 0; i < node.tri_count; ++i) {
                    int tri_idx = mesh.bvh_tri_indices[node.tri_start + i];
                    const auto& f = mesh.faces[tri_idx];
                    double t, u, v;
                    if (ray_intersects_tri(p, rd, mesh.verts[f[0]], mesh.verts[f[1]], mesh.verts[f[2]], t, u, v)) {
                        if (t < min_t) {
                            min_t = t;
                            hit_tri = tri_idx;
                            if (u < 1e-4 || v < 1e-4 || (1.0 - u - v) < 1e-4) {
                                edge_hit = true;
                            } else {
                                edge_hit = false;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else {
                stack.push_back(node.left);
                stack.push_back(node.right);
            }
        }
        
        if (hit_tri != -1) {
            if (edge_hit) continue;
            double d = dot(rd, mesh.normals[hit_tri]);
            return d > 0;
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    }
    return false;
}

void find_overlaps(const BVHNode& nodeA, const Mesh& meshA, const BVHNode& nodeB, const Mesh& meshB, std::vector<std::pair<int, int>>& overlaps) {
    if (!nodeA.box.overlaps(nodeB.box)) return;
    
    if (nodeA.left == -1 && nodeB.left == -1) {
        for (int i = 0; i < nodeA.tri_count; ++i) {
            for (int j = 0; j < nodeB.tri_count; ++j) {
                overlaps.push_back({meshA.bvh_tri_indices[nodeA.tri_start + i], meshB.bvh_tri_indices[nodeB.tri_start + j]});
            }
        }
    } else if (nodeA.left == -1) {
        find_overlaps(nodeA, meshA, meshB.bvh_nodes[nodeB.left], meshB, overlaps);
        find_overlaps(nodeA, meshA, meshB.bvh_nodes[nodeB.right], meshB, overlaps);
    } else if (nodeB.left == -1) {
        find_overlaps(meshA.bvh_nodes[nodeA.left], meshA, nodeB, meshB, overlaps);
        find_overlaps(meshA.bvh_nodes[nodeA.right], meshA, nodeB, meshB, overlaps);
    } else {
        Vector3 extA = nodeA.box.max - nodeA.box.min;
        Vector3 extB = nodeB.box.max - nodeB.box.min;
        double sizeA = extA.x + extA.y + extA.z;
        double sizeB = extB.x + extB.y + extB.z;
        if (sizeA > sizeB) {
            find_overlaps(meshA.bvh_nodes[nodeA.left], meshA, nodeB, meshB, overlaps);
            find_overlaps(meshA.bvh_nodes[nodeA.right], meshA, nodeB, meshB, overlaps);
        } else {
            find_overlaps(nodeA, meshA, meshB.bvh_nodes[nodeB.left], meshB, overlaps);
            find_overlaps(nodeA, meshA, meshB.bvh_nodes[nodeB.right], meshB, overlaps);
        }
    }
}

bool tri_tri_intersect(const Vector3& V0, const Vector3& V1, const Vector3& V2,
                       const Vector3& U0, const Vector3& U1, const Vector3& U2) {
    Vector3 N_V = cross(V1 - V0, V2 - V0);
    double d_V = -dot(N_V, V0);
    
    double du0 = dot(N_V, U0) + d_V;
    double du1 = dot(N_V, U1) + d_V;
    double du2 = dot(N_V, U2) + d_V;
    
    if (du0 >= -1e-9 && du1 >= -1e-9 && du2 >= -1e-9) return false;
    if (du0 <= 1e-9 && du1 <= 1e-9 && du2 <= 1e-9) return false;
    
    Vector3 N_U = cross(U1 - U0, U2 - U0);
    double d_U = -dot(N_U, U0);
    
    double dv0 = dot(N_U, V0) + d_U;
    double dv1 = dot(N_U, V1) + d_U;
    double dv2 = dot(N_U, V2) + d_U;
    
    if (dv0 >= -1e-9 && dv1 >= -1e-9 && dv2 >= -1e-9) return false;
    if (dv0 <= 1e-9 && dv1 <= 1e-9 && dv2 <= 1e-9) return false;
    
    Vector3 D = cross(N_V, N_U);
    if (length_squared(D) < 1e-12 * length_squared(N_V) * length_squared(N_U)) {
        return true; 
    }
    
    auto get_interval = [&](const Vector3& p0, const Vector3& p1, const Vector3& p2, double d0, double d1, double d2, double& t_min, double& t_max) {
        Vector3 p_alone, p_other1, p_other2;
        double d_alone, d_other1, d_other2;
        if (d0 * d1 > 0) { p_alone = p2; d_alone = d2; p_other1 = p0; d_other1 = d0; p_other2 = p1; d_other2 = d1; }
        else if (d0 * d2 > 0) { p_alone = p1; d_alone = d1; p_other1 = p0; d_other1 = d0; p_other2 = p2; d_other2 = d2; }
        else { p_alone = p0; d_alone = d0; p_other1 = p1; d_other1 = d1; p_other2 = p2; d_other2 = d2; }
        
        double t1 = d_alone / (d_alone - d_other1);
        Vector3 i1 = p_alone + (p_other1 - p_alone) * t1;
        double t2 = d_alone / (d_alone - d_other2);
        Vector3 i2 = p_alone + (p_other2 - p_alone) * t2;
        
        double proj1 = dot(D, i1);
        double proj2 = dot(D, i2);
        t_min = std::min(proj1, proj2);
        t_max = std::max(proj1, proj2);
    };
    
    double tV_min, tV_max;
    get_interval(V0, V1, V2, dv0, dv1, dv2, tV_min, tV_max);
    
    double tU_min, tU_max;
    get_interval(U0, U1, U2, du0, du1, du2, tU_min, tU_max);
    
    if (tV_max < tU_min || tU_max < tV_min) return false;
    
    return true;
}

struct Plane {
    Vector3 n;
    double d;
};

void clean_poly(std::vector<Vector3>& p) {
    if (p.size() < 3) return;
    std::vector<Vector3> np;
    np.push_back(p[0]);
    for (size_t i = 1; i < p.size(); ++i) {
        if (length_squared(p[i] - np.back()) > 1e-14) {
            np.push_back(p[i]);
        }
    }
    if (np.size() >= 2 && length_squared(np.front() - np.back()) <= 1e-14) {
        np.pop_back();
    }
    p = np;
}

double poly_area(const std::vector<Vector3>& p, const Vector3& n) {
    Vector3 area(0,0,0);
    for(size_t i=0; i<p.size(); ++i){
        area = area + cross(p[i], p[(i+1)%p.size()]);
    }
    return std::abs(dot(area, n)) * 0.5;
}

void split_polygon(const vector<Vector3>& poly, const Plane& plane, vector<vector<Vector3>>& out_polys) {
    if (poly.size() < 3) return;
    vector<double> dists(poly.size());
    int front_count = 0, back_count = 0;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < poly.size(); ++i) {
        dists[i] = dot(poly[i], plane.n) + plane.d;
        if (dists[i] > 1e-8) front_count++;
        else if (dists[i] < -1e-8) back_count++;
        else dists[i] = 0.0;
    }
    
    if (back_count == 0 || front_count == 0) {
        out_polys.push_back(poly);
        return;
    }
    
    vector<Vector3> front, back;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < poly.size(); ++i) {
        size_t j = (i + 1) % poly.size();
        if (dists[i] >= 0) front.push_back(poly[i]);
        if (dists[i] <= 0) back.push_back(poly[i]);
        
        if ((dists[i] > 0 && dists[j] < 0) || (dists[i] < 0 && dists[j] > 0)) {
            double t = dists[i] / (dists[i] - dists[j]);
            Vector3 p = poly[i] + (poly[j] - poly[i]) * t;
            front.push_back(p);
            back.push_back(p);
        }
    }
    clean_poly(front);
    clean_poly(back);
    if (front.size() >= 3) out_polys.push_back(front);
    if (back.size() >= 3) out_polys.push_back(back);
}

bool point_in_triangle(const Vector3& p, const Vector3& a, const Vector3& b, const Vector3& c) {
    Vector3 v0 = c - a;
    Vector3 v1 = b - a;
    Vector3 v2 = p - a;

    double dot00 = dot(v0, v0);
    double dot01 = dot(v0, v1);
    double dot02 = dot(v0, v2);
    double dot11 = dot(v1, v1);
    double dot12 = dot(v1, v2);

    double invDenom = 1.0 / (dot00 * dot11 - dot01 * dot01);
    double u = (dot11 * dot02 - dot01 * dot12) * invDenom;
    double v = (dot00 * dot12 - dot01 * dot02) * invDenom;

    return (u >= -1e-6) && (v >= -1e-6) && (u + v <= 1.0 + 1e-6);
}

struct SpatialHash {
    struct Vertex {
        Vector3 p;
        int idx;
    };
    std::unordered_map<int64_t, std::vector<Vertex>> map;
    std::vector<Vector3> verts;
    double cell_size = 1e-6;
    
    int64_t hash(int64_t x, int64_t y, int64_t z) {
        return (x * 73856093) ^ (y * 19349663) ^ (z * 83492791);
    }
    
    int add(const Vector3& v) {
        int64_t bx = static_cast<int64_t>(std::floor(v.x / cell_size));
        int64_t by = static_cast<int64_t>(std::floor(v.y / cell_size));
        int64_t bz = static_cast<int64_t>(std::floor(v.z / cell_size));
        
        int best_idx = -1;
        double min_dist = cell_size * cell_size * 4;
        
        for (int64_t dx = -1; dx <= 1; ++dx) {
            for (int64_t dy = -1; dy <= 1; ++dy) {
                for (int64_t dz = -1; dz <= 1; ++dz) {
                    int64_t h = hash(bx + dx, by + dy, bz + dz);
                    auto it = map.find(h);
                    if (it != map.end()) {
                        for (const auto& vertex : it->second) {
                            double dist = length_squared(vertex.p - v);
                            if (dist < min_dist) {
                                min_dist = dist;
                                best_idx = vertex.idx;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        if (best_idx != -1 && min_dist < cell_size * cell_size) {
            return best_idx;
        }
        
        int idx = verts.size();
        verts.push_back(v);
        map[hash(bx, by, bz)].push_back({v, idx});
        return idx;
    }
};

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(NULL);
    
    int VA, FA, VB, FB;
    if (!(cin >> VA >> FA >> VB >> FB)) return 0;
    
    Mesh meshA;
    meshA.verts.resize(VA);
    for(int i=0; i<VA; ++i) cin >> meshA.verts[i].x >> meshA.verts[i].y >> meshA.verts[i].z;
    meshA.faces.resize(FA);
    for(int i=0; i<FA; ++i) cin >> meshA.faces[i][0] >> meshA.faces[i][1] >> meshA.faces[i][2];
    
    Mesh meshB;
    meshB.verts.resize(VB);
    for(int i=0; i<VB; ++i) cin >> meshB.verts[i].x >> meshB.verts[i].y >> meshB.verts[i].z;
    meshB.faces.resize(FB);
    for(int i=0; i<FB; ++i) cin >> meshB.faces[i][0] >> meshB.faces[i][1] >> meshB.faces[i][2];
    
    meshA.build();
    meshB.build();
    
    std::vector<std::pair<int, int>> overlaps;
    if (!meshA.bvh_nodes.empty() && !meshB.bvh_nodes.empty()) {
        find_overlaps(meshA.bvh_nodes[0], meshA, meshB.bvh_nodes[0], meshB, overlaps);
    }
    
    std::vector<std::vector<int>> A_to_B(FA);
    std::vector<std::vector<int>> B_to_A(FB);
    for (auto& p : overlaps) {
        A_to_B[p.first].push_back(p.second);
        B_to_A[p.second].push_back(p.first);
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < FA; ++i) {
        std::sort(A_to_B[i].begin(), A_to_B[i].end());
        A_to_B[i].erase(std::unique(A_to_B[i].begin(), A_to_B[i].end()), A_to_B[i].end());
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < FB; ++i) {
        std::sort(B_to_A[i].begin(), B_to_A[i].end());
        B_to_A[i].erase(std::unique(B_to_A[i].begin(), B_to_A[i].end()), B_to_A[i].end());
    }
    
    std::vector<std::vector<std::array<Vector3, 3>>> thread_outA(FA);
    std::vector<int> A_indices(FA);
    for(int i=0; i<FA; ++i) A_indices[i] = i;
    
    std::for_each(std::execution::par, A_indices.begin(), A_indices.end(), [&](int triA_idx) {
        const auto& fA = meshA.faces[triA_idx];
        Vector3 vA0 = meshA.verts[fA[0]];
        Vector3 vA1 = meshA.verts[fA[1]];
        Vector3 vA2 = meshA.verts[fA[2]];
        Vector3 N_A = meshA.normals[triA_idx];
        
        std::vector<Plane> clip_planes;
        for (int triB_idx : A_to_B[triA_idx]) {
            const auto& fB = meshB.faces[triB_idx];
            Vector3 vB0 = meshB.verts[fB[0]];
            Vector3 vB1 = meshB.verts[fB[1]];
            Vector3 vB2 = meshB.verts[fB[2]];
            Vector3 N_B = meshB.normals[triB_idx];
            
            if (tri_tri_intersect(vA0, vA1, vA2, vB0, vB1, vB2)) {
                if (std::abs(dot(N_A, N_B)) > 1 - 1e-6 && std::abs(dot(N_A, vB0 - vA0)) < 1e-6) {
                    Plane p1; p1.n = normalize(cross(N_A, vB1 - vB0)); p1.d = -dot(p1.n, vB0);
                    Plane p2; p2.n = normalize(cross(N_A, vB2 - vB1)); p2.d = -dot(p2.n, vB1);
                    Plane p3; p3.n = normalize(cross(N_A, vB0 - vB2)); p3.d = -dot(p3.n, vB2);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p1);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p2);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p3);
                } else {
                    Plane p; p.n = N_B; p.d = -dot(N_B, vB0);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p);
                }
            }
        }
        
        std::vector<std::vector<Vector3>> polys = { {vA0, vA1, vA2} };
        for (const auto& plane : clip_planes) {
            std::vector<std::vector<Vector3>> next_polys;
            for (const auto& poly : polys) {
                split_polygon(poly, plane, next_polys);
            }
            polys = next_polys;
        }
        
        for (const auto& poly : polys) {
            if (poly_area(poly, N_A) < 1e-10) continue;
            Vector3 C(0,0,0);
            for (const auto& p : poly) C = C + p;
            C = C * (1.0 / poly.size());
            
            Vector3 P_ray = C + N_A * 1e-5;
            if (!is_inside(meshB, P_ray)) {
                for (size_t i = 1; i < poly.size() - 1; ++i) {
                    thread_outA[triA_idx].push_back({poly[0], poly[i], poly[i+1]});
                }
            }
        }
    });
    
    std::vector<std::vector<std::array<Vector3, 3>>> thread_outB(FB);
    std::vector<int> B_indices(FB);
    for(int i=0; i<FB; ++i) B_indices[i] = i;
    
    std::for_each(std::execution::par, B_indices.begin(), B_indices.end(), [&](int triB_idx) {
        const auto& fB = meshB.faces[triB_idx];
        Vector3 vB0 = meshB.verts[fB[0]];
        Vector3 vB1 = meshB.verts[fB[1]];
        Vector3 vB2 = meshB.verts[fB[2]];
        Vector3 N_B = meshB.normals[triB_idx];
        
        std::vector<Plane> clip_planes;
        for (int triA_idx : B_to_A[triB_idx]) {
            const auto& fA = meshA.faces[triA_idx];
            Vector3 vA0 = meshA.verts[fA[0]];
            Vector3 vA1 = meshA.verts[fA[1]];
            Vector3 vA2 = meshA.verts[fA[2]];
            Vector3 N_A = meshA.normals[triA_idx];
            
            if (tri_tri_intersect(vB0, vB1, vB2, vA0, vA1, vA2)) {
                if (std::abs(dot(N_B, N_A)) > 1 - 1e-6 && std::abs(dot(N_B, vA0 - vB0)) < 1e-6) {
                    Plane p1; p1.n = normalize(cross(N_B, vA1 - vA0)); p1.d = -dot(p1.n, vA0);
                    Plane p2; p2.n = normalize(cross(N_B, vA2 - vA1)); p2.d = -dot(p2.n, vA1);
                    Plane p3; p3.n = normalize(cross(N_B, vA0 - vA2)); p3.d = -dot(p3.n, vA2);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p1);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p2);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p3);
                } else {
                    Plane p; p.n = N_A; p.d = -dot(N_A, vA0);
                    clip_planes.push_back(p);
                }
            }
        }
        
        std::vector<std::vector<Vector3>> polys = { {vB0, vB1, vB2} };
        for (const auto& plane : clip_planes) {
            std::vector<std::vector<Vector3>> next_polys;
            for (const auto& poly : polys) {
                split_polygon(poly, plane, next_polys);
            }
            polys = next_polys;
        }
        
        for (const auto& poly : polys) {
            if (poly_area(poly, N_B) < 1e-10) continue;
            Vector3 C(0,0,0);
            for (const auto& p : poly) C = C + p;
            C = C * (1.0 / poly.size());
            
            bool duplicate = false;
            for (int triA_idx : B_to_A[triB_idx]) {
                const auto& fA = meshA.faces[triA_idx];
                if (dot(meshA.normals[triA_idx], N_B) > 1 - 1e-6) {
                    if (std::abs(dot(meshA.normals[triA_idx], C - meshA.verts[fA[0]])) < 1e-6) {
                        if (point_in_triangle(C, meshA.verts[fA[0]], meshA.verts[fA[1]], meshA.verts[fA[2]])) {
                            duplicate = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            if (duplicate) continue;
            
            Vector3 P_ray = C + N_B * 1e-5;
            if (!is_inside(meshA, P_ray)) {
                for (size_t i = 1; i < poly.size() - 1; ++i) {
                    thread_outB[triB_idx].push_back({poly[0], poly[i], poly[i+1]});
                }
            }
        }
    });
    
    SpatialHash hash;
    std::vector<std::array<int, 3>> final_faces;
    
    auto add_triangle = [&](const std::array<Vector3, 3>& t) {
        int i0 = hash.add(t[0]);
        int i1 = hash.add(t[1]);
        int i2 = hash.add(t[2]);
        if (i0 != i1 && i1 != i2 && i2 != i0) {
            final_faces.push_back({i0, i1, i2});
        }
    };
    
    for (int i = 0; i < FA; ++i) {
        for (const auto& t : thread_outA[i]) add_triangle(t);
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < FB; ++i) {
        for (const auto& t : thread_outB[i]) add_triangle(t);
    }
    
    cout << hash.verts.size() << " " << final_faces.size() << "\n";
    for (const auto& v : hash.verts) {
        cout << fixed << setprecision(8) << v.x << " " << v.y << " " << v.z << "\n";
    }
    for (const auto& f : final_faces) {
        cout << f[0] << " " << f[1] << " " << f[2] << "\n";
    }
    
    return 0;
}

Test 8: Maze Solver (Rust) Score: 14.00 / 14
Typical Prompt:
You are writing a maze solver in Rust that must handle ANY maze complexity from trivial to ludicrous scale.

Your program will be tested with mazes ranging from 5x5 to 50000x50000.
The same program must work efficiently across ALL scales.

**Maze format:**
- 'A' = Start position
- 'B' = Goal/End position
- '#' = Wall (cannot pass through)
- ' ' (space) = Open path (can walk through)

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: H W (height and width)
Next H lines: the maze row strings (each W characters)

**Output format (stdout):**
Line 1: N (number of steps in path)
Next N lines: x y (0-indexed coordinates from top-left)
Path should include both start (A) and end (B) positions.
Movement is only up/down/left/right (no diagonals).
Output nothing (or 0) if no path exists.

**Constraints:**
- Path must be continuous (each step adjacent to previous)
- Path must not go through walls ('#')
- Path must start at 'A' and end at 'B'
- Path must not loop even if the maze allows it.
- If multiple solutions exist, return any one.

**Environment:**
Platform: Windows 11 (build 10.0.26200)
Architecture: AMD64
CPU: Intel64 Family 6 Model 158 Stepping 10, GenuineIntel

use std::io::{self, BufRead, Read, Write};
use std::collections::VecDeque;

struct FastOut<W: Write> {
    writer: W,
    buf: Vec<u8>,
}

impl<W: Write> FastOut<W> {
    fn new(writer: W) -> Self {
        Self {
            writer,
            buf: Vec::with_capacity(128 * 1024),
        }
    }

    fn write_u32(&mut self, mut n: u32) {
        if n == 0 {
            self.push(b'0');
            return;
        }
        let mut temp = [0u8; 10];
        let mut idx = 10;
        while n > 0 {
            idx -= 1;
            temp[idx] = b'0' + (n % 10) as u8;
            n /= 10;
        }
        let slice = &temp[idx..];
        if self.buf.len() + slice.len() > self.buf.capacity() {
            self.writer.write_all(&self.buf).unwrap();
            self.buf.clear();
        }
        self.buf.extend_from_slice(slice);
    }

    fn push(&mut self, b: u8) {
        if self.buf.len() == self.buf.capacity() {
            self.writer.write_all(&self.buf).unwrap();
            self.buf.clear();
        }
        self.buf.push(b);
    }

    fn flush(&mut self) {
        if !self.buf.is_empty() {
            self.writer.write_all(&self.buf).unwrap();
            self.buf.clear();
        }
    }
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut handle = stdin.lock();

    let mut header = String::new();
    handle.read_line(&mut header).unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<usize> = header.trim().split_whitespace().map(|s| s.parse().unwrap()).collect();
    if parts.len() < 2 { return; }
    let h = parts[0];
    let w = parts[1];

    let total_cells = h * w;
    let mut grid = Vec::with_capacity(total_cells);
    let mut start_idx = u32::MAX;
    let mut end_idx = u32::MAX;

    // Use a heap-allocated buffer to prevent stack overflow on Windows (MSVC default stack size is 1MB)
    let mut buffer = vec![0u8; 1024 * 1024];
    while let Ok(n) = handle.read(&mut buffer) {
        if n == 0 { break; }
        for i in 0..n {
            let b = buffer[i];
            if b != b'\n' && b != b'\r' {
                if b == b'A' {
                    start_idx = grid.len() as u32;
                } else if b == b'B' {
                    end_idx = grid.len() as u32;
                }
                grid.push(b);
                if grid.len() == total_cells {
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        if grid.len() == total_cells {
            break;
        }
    }

    if start_idx == u32::MAX || end_idx == u32::MAX {
        println!("0");
        return;
    }
    if start_idx == end_idx {
        println!("1");
        println!("{} {}", start_idx % (w as u32), start_idx / (w as u32));
        return;
    }

    let w32 = w as u32;
    let h32 = h as u32;

    let mut queue = VecDeque::new();
    queue.push_back(start_idx);

    let mut found = false;
    let mut before_end = u32::MAX;

    // BFS loop using grid for storing parent directions to save massive amounts of memory
    while let Some(curr) = queue.pop_front() {
        let r = curr / w32;
        let c = curr % w32;

        // Up
        if r > 0 {
            let next = curr - w32;
            let b = unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked(next as usize) };
            if b == b'B' {
                found = true;
                before_end = curr;
                break;
            } else if b == b' ' {
                unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked_mut(next as usize) = b'D' };
                queue.push_back(next);
            }
        }
        // Down
        if r + 1 < h32 {
            let next = curr + w32;
            let b = unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked(next as usize) };
            if b == b'B' {
                found = true;
                before_end = curr;
                break;
            } else if b == b' ' {
                unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked_mut(next as usize) = b'U' };
                queue.push_back(next);
            }
        }
        // Left
        if c > 0 {
            let next = curr - 1;
            let b = unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked(next as usize) };
            if b == b'B' {
                found = true;
                before_end = curr;
                break;
            } else if b == b' ' {
                unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked_mut(next as usize) = b'R' };
                queue.push_back(next);
            }
        }
        // Right
        if c + 1 < w32 {
            let next = curr + 1;
            let b = unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked(next as usize) };
            if b == b'B' {
                found = true;
                before_end = curr;
                break;
            } else if b == b' ' {
                unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked_mut(next as usize) = b'L' };
                queue.push_back(next);
            }
        }
    }

    let stdout = io::stdout();
    let mut out = FastOut::new(stdout.lock());

    if found {
        let mut path = Vec::new();
        path.push(end_idx);
        let mut current = before_end;
        while current != start_idx {
            path.push(current);
            let back_dir = unsafe { *grid.get_unchecked(current as usize) };
            if back_dir == b'U' {
                current -= w32;
            } else if back_dir == b'D' {
                current += w32;
            } else if back_dir == b'L' {
                current -= 1;
            } else if back_dir == b'R' {
                current += 1;
            } else {
                panic!("Broken path");
            }
        }
        path.push(start_idx);

        out.write_u32(path.len() as u32);
        out.push(b'\n');
        // Reconstruct path in correct order natively
        for &node in path.iter().rev() {
            out.write_u32(node % w32); // x
            out.push(b' ');
            out.write_u32(node / w32); // y
            out.push(b'\n');
        }
    } else {
        out.write_u32(0);
        out.push(b'\n');
    }
    out.flush();
}

Test 9: 1D Cutting Stock - Minimum Waste (C#) Score: 0.00 / 15
Typical Prompt:
You are solving the 1D Cutting Stock Problem in C#.

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: N stock_length
Line 2: N cut lengths separated by spaces

**Output format (stdout):**
Line 1: num_stocks
Next num_stocks lines: space-separated cut indices assigned to that stock (0-indexed)

**Example:**
For cuts=[30, 40, 50] and stock_length=100:
Input:
3 100
30 40 50

Output:
2
0 1
2

**Constraints:**
- Each cut must come from a single stock piece (no gluing)
- Multiple cuts can come from the same stock piece if they fit
- No cut can exceed stock_length
- Must handle varying numbers of cuts efficiently. You can use
multiple threads, you can micro-optimise code, you can write clever algorithms,
whatever it takes to handle the problem and solve it within 5 minutes even if
there are millions of cuts.

Given fixed-length stock material and a shopping list of smaller pieces to cut, use as few stock pieces as possible. Every requested piece must be cut from somewhere, but any leftover material is wasted — so packing the cuts tightly matters.

This is essentially a bin-packing problem and is NP-hard. Subpasses scale from a handful of cuts up to millions, forcing the AI to write code that is both correct and fast. The baseline uses a simple first-fit-decreasing heuristic.

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

class FastScanner
{
    private Stream stream;
    private byte[] buffer = new byte[1024 * 1024];
    private int head;
    private int tail;

    public FastScanner(Stream stream)
    {
        this.stream = stream;
    }

    public long ReadLong()
    {
        int c = Read();
        while (c <= ' ')
        {
            if (c == -1) return -1;
            c = Read();
        }
        long res = 0;
        while (c > ' ')
        {
            res = res * 10 + c - '0';
            c = Read();
        }
        return res;
    }

    private int Read()
    {
        if (head >= tail)
        {
            head = 0;
            tail = stream.Read(buffer, 0, buffer.Length);
            if (tail == 0) return -1;
        }
        return buffer[head++];
    }
}

class FastWriter : IDisposable
{
    private Stream stream;
    private byte[] buffer = new byte[1024 * 1024];
    private int pos;

    public FastWriter(Stream stream)
    {
        this.stream = stream;
    }

    public void Write(int value)
    {
        if (pos + 12 > buffer.Length) Flush();
        if (value == 0)
        {
            buffer[pos++] = (byte)'0';
            return;
        }
        if (value < 0)
        {
            buffer[pos++] = (byte)'-';
            value = -value;
        }
        int len = 0;
        int temp = value;
        while (temp > 0)
        {
            temp /= 10;
            len++;
        }
        for (int i = len - 1; i >= 0; i--)
        {
            buffer[pos + i] = (byte)('0' + (value % 10));
            value /= 10;
        }
        pos += len;
    }

    public void WriteSpace()
    {
        if (pos + 1 > buffer.Length) Flush();
        buffer[pos++] = (byte)' ';
    }

    public void WriteLine()
    {
        if (pos + 1 > buffer.Length) Flush();
        buffer[pos++] = (byte)'\n';
    }

    public void Flush()
    {
        if (pos > 0)
        {
            stream.Write(buffer, 0, pos);
            pos = 0;
        }
    }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        Flush();
    }
}

class Program
{
    struct Cut : IComparable<Cut>
    {
        public long Length;
        public int Idx;
        public int CompareTo(Cut other)
        {
            int c = other.Length.CompareTo(this.Length);
            if (c == 0) return this.Idx.CompareTo(other.Idx);
            return c;
        }
    }

    class Bin : IComparable<Bin>
    {
        public long Capacity;
        public int Id;
        public int CompareTo(Bin other)
        {
            int c = this.Capacity.CompareTo(other.Capacity);
            if (c == 0) return this.Id.CompareTo(other.Id);
            return c;
        }
    }

    class Result
    {
        public int BinsUsed;
        public int[] Head;
        public int[] Next;

        public void Print()
        {
            using (FastWriter writer = new FastWriter(Console.OpenStandardOutput()))
            {
                writer.Write(BinsUsed);
                writer.WriteLine();
                for (int i = 0; i < BinsUsed; i++)
                {
                    int curr = Head[i];
                    bool first = true;
                    while (curr != -1)
                    {
                        if (!first) writer.WriteSpace();
                        writer.Write(curr);
                        first = false;
                        curr = Next[curr];
                    }
                    writer.WriteLine();
                }
            }
        }
    }

    static void Main()
    {
        using (Stream stdin = Console.OpenStandardInput())
        {
            FastScanner scanner = new FastScanner(stdin);
            long n_long = scanner.ReadLong();
            if (n_long <= 0) return;
            int N = (int)n_long;
            long stockLength = scanner.ReadLong();

            Cut[] items = new Cut[N];
            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
            {
                items[i] = new Cut { Length = scanner.ReadLong(), Idx = i };
            }

            Array.Sort(items);

            Task<Result> ffdTask = Task.Run(() => RunFFD(items, stockLength, N));
            Task<Result> bfdTask = Task.Run(() => RunBFD(items, stockLength, N));

            Task.WaitAll(ffdTask, bfdTask);

            Result best = ffdTask.Result.BinsUsed <= bfdTask.Result.BinsUsed ? ffdTask.Result : bfdTask.Result;
            best.Print();
        }
    }

    static Result RunFFD(Cut[] items, long stockLength, int N)
    {
        int M = 1;
        while (M < N) M *= 2;

        long[] tree = new long[2 * M];
        for (int i = 0; i < M; i++)
        {
            if (i < N) tree[M + i] = stockLength;
            else tree[M + i] = 0;
        }
        for (int i = M - 1; i > 0; i--)
        {
            tree[i] = Math.Max(tree[2 * i], tree[2 * i + 1]);
        }

        int[] head = new int[N];
        int[] tail = new int[N];
        int[] next = new int[N];
        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) head[i] = -1;

        int maxBinIndex = -1;

        foreach (var item in items)
        {
            long val = item.Length;
            if (tree[1] < val) throw new Exception("Cannot fit item");

            int node = 1;
            while (node < M)
            {
                if (tree[2 * node] >= val) node = 2 * node;
                else node = 2 * node + 1;
            }

            tree[node] -= val;
            int binIndex = node - M;
            if (binIndex > maxBinIndex) maxBinIndex = binIndex;

            node /= 2;
            while (node > 0)
            {
                tree[node] = Math.Max(tree[2 * node], tree[2 * node + 1]);
                node /= 2;
            }

            int idx = item.Idx;
            if (head[binIndex] == -1)
            {
                head[binIndex] = idx;
                tail[binIndex] = idx;
            }
            else
            {
                next[tail[binIndex]] = idx;
                tail[binIndex] = idx;
            }
            next[idx] = -1;
        }

        return new Result
        {
            BinsUsed = maxBinIndex + 1,
            Head = head,
            Next = next
        };
    }

    static Result RunBFD(Cut[] items, long stockLength, int N)
    {
        SortedSet<Bin> availableBins = new SortedSet<Bin>();
        Bin dummyMin = new Bin { Capacity = 0, Id = -1 };
        Bin dummyMax = new Bin { Capacity = long.MaxValue, Id = int.MaxValue };

        int[] head = new int[N];
        int[] tail = new int[N];
        int[] next = new int[N];
        for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) head[i] = -1;

        int nextBinId = 0;

        foreach (var item in items)
        {
            long val = item.Length;
            dummyMin.Capacity = val;

            var view = availableBins.GetViewBetween(dummyMin, dummyMax);
            Bin bestBin = view.Min;

            if (bestBin == null)
            {
                bestBin = new Bin { Capacity = stockLength, Id = nextBinId++ };
            }
            else
            {
                availableBins.Remove(bestBin);
            }

            bestBin.Capacity -= val;
            availableBins.Add(bestBin);

            int binIndex = bestBin.Id;
            int idx = item.Idx;
            if (head[binIndex] == -1)
            {
                head[binIndex] = idx;
                tail[binIndex] = idx;
            }
            else
            {
                next[tail[binIndex]] = idx;
                tail[binIndex] = idx;
            }
            next[idx] = -1;
        }

        return new Result
        {
            BinsUsed = nextBinId,
            Head = head,
            Next = next
        };
    }
}

Test 10: 2D Cutting Stock - Rectangle Packing (C++) Score: 0.00 / 13
Typical Prompt:
You are solving the 2D Cutting Stock Problem (Rectangle Bin Packing) in C++.

Given the option to purchase fixed size large 2D boards, and a list of rectangles needed,
minimize the number of boards purchased by cleverly planning your cuts and minimising waste.

You must write a C++ solver that can handle ANY problem size from trivial to ludicrous scale:
- **Trivial**: 4-8 rectangles, 100x100-200x150 boards
- **Ludicrous**: 500-50000 rectangles, 2000x2000-10000x10000 boards

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: N board_width board_height
Next N lines: w h (rectangle dimensions)

**Output format (stdout):**
Line 1: num_boards
Next N lines: board_index x y rotated (one per rectangle, rotated is 0 or 1)

**Critical Requirements:**
1. **Scalability**: Your algorithm must adapt based on problem size and board dimensions
2. **Performance**: Must complete within 30 seconds even for 50000 rectangles
3. **Quality**: Minimize number of boards used while producing valid placements

**Constraints:**
- Rectangles may be rotated 90° if it helps
- No overlapping allowed
- Rectangles must not exceed board boundaries

**Environment:**
Platform: Windows 11 (build 10.0.26200)
Architecture: AMD64
CPU: Intel64 Family 6 Model 158 Stepping 10, GenuineIntel
Core count: 12
Memory: 31.93 GB
SIMD: AVX, AVX2, SSE, SSE2, SSE3, SSE4.1, SSE4.2, SSSE3
SIMD detail: AVX=yes, AVX-512F=no, AVX2=yes, SSE=yes, SSE2=yes, SSE3=yes, SSE4.1=yes, SSE4.2=yes, SSSE3=yes

2D Cutting Stock - 4 rectangles, 100x100 board

I have implemented a highly optimized C++ solution and saved it to `solution.cpp`.

### Solution Overview
The implementation uses a robust **MaxRects** bin packing algorithm paired with **First Fit Decreasing** heuristics to maximize the utilization of large boards efficiently:

1. **MaxRects BSSF**: The core placement logic uses "Best Short Side Fit" which tightly fits rectangles into the optimal available corners of a board, producing excellent bounds and minimal space waste.
2. **First Fit Board Allocation**: Instead of generating a massive multi-dimensional index, the algorithm iterates over previously opened boards to find the best fit before allocating a new board.
3. **`O(1)` Filtering**: For ludicrous problem sizes (e.g., 50,000 rectangles, hundreds of boards), the main bottleneck is iterating over large open nodes within fully-packed bins. I added an `O(1)` check that maintains the maximum/minimum unallocated spatial dimension bounds of a board (`maxFreeMaxDim` and `maxFreeMinDim`), rejecting impossible insertions instantly rather than verifying thousands of free internal nodes inside a board unnecessarily. 
4. **Time-Bound Heuristics**: The code runs up to 6 different optimal heuristic sorting variations (Area desc, Max/Min dim desc, Perimeter, etc.) inside the allowed 30-second timeframe to guarantee you always receive the best layout configuration possible.
5. **Standard Library Constraints**: Strictly uses C++ standard libraries (`<iostream>`, `<vector>`, `<algorithm>`, `<chrono>`) and conforms to the C++20 specifications suitable for MSVC cl. Optimized stdout mapping is applied for safe rendering of 50,000 outputs efficiently.

Typical Prompt:
You are solving a 2D Polygon Cutting Stock Problem in Rust.

**The Challenge:**
Your program will be tested with problems ranging from 2 simple pieces to 5000+ complex polygons.
The same program must work efficiently across ALL scales.

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: SV NP (number of stock polygon vertices, number of pieces)
Next SV lines: x y (stock polygon vertices)
For each piece:
Line: PV (number of vertices in this piece)
Next PV lines: x y (piece polygon vertices)

**Output format (stdout):**
Line 1: num_stocks
Next NP lines: stock_index x y rotation (one per piece)
stock_index: 0-indexed stock polygon
x y: translation to apply
rotation: angle in radians

1. **Scalability**: Your algorithm must adapt based on number and complexity of pieces
2. **Performance**: Must complete within 5 minutes even for 5000+ complex pieces
3. **Quality**: Minimize stock usage while ensuring valid placements

**Constraints:**
- Each placed piece must fit entirely within the stock polygon
- Pieces on same stock must not overlap
- Pieces may be rotated to any angle

The AI must handle polygon geometry (containment, intersection, rotation) and plan efficient layouts. Subpasses increase the number and complexity of the pieces. The baseline uses a simple greedy placement strategy.

use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}
