use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

Polygon Cutting - 50 pieces from 500x500

View Code (9446 chars)
use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

View Code (9446 chars)
use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();

    for _ in 0..sv {

        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };

                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);

        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });

    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;

    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

View Code (9446 chars)
use std::io::{self, BufRead};
use std::f64::consts::PI;

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Point {
    x: f64,
    y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Polygon {
    vertices: Vec<Point>,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct AABB {
    min_x: f64,
    max_x: f64,
    min_y: f64,
    max_y: f64,
}

#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
struct Edge {
    p1: Point,
    p2: Point,
    aabb: AABB,
}

fn get_aabb(poly: &Polygon) -> AABB {
    let mut min_x = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_x = f64::MIN;
    let mut min_y = f64::MAX;
    let mut max_y = f64::MIN;
    for p in &poly.vertices {
        if p.x < min_x { min_x = p.x; }
        if p.x > max_x { max_x = p.x; }
        if p.y < min_y { min_y = p.y; }
        if p.y > max_y { max_y = p.y; }
    }
    AABB { min_x, max_x, min_y, max_y }
}

fn build_edges(poly: &Polygon) -> Vec<Edge> {
    let mut edges = Vec::with_capacity(poly.vertices.len());
    for i in 0..poly.vertices.len() {
        let p1 = &poly.vertices[i];
        let p2 = &poly.vertices[(i + 1) % poly.vertices.len()];
        edges.push(Edge {
            p1: p1.clone(),
            p2: p2.clone(),
            aabb: AABB {
                min_x: p1.x.min(p2.x),
                max_x: p1.x.max(p2.x),
                min_y: p1.y.min(p2.y),
                max_y: p1.y.max(p2.y),
            }
        });
    }
    edges
}

fn aabb_overlap(a: &AABB, b: &AABB) -> bool {
    !(a.max_x < b.min_x || a.min_x > b.max_x || a.max_y < b.min_y || a.min_y > b.max_y)
}

fn rotate(poly: &Polygon, angle: f64) -> Polygon {
    let cos_a = angle.cos();
    let sin_a = angle.sin();
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point {
            x: p.x * cos_a - p.y * sin_a,
            y: p.x * sin_a + p.y * cos_a,
        }).collect(),
    }
}

fn translate(poly: &Polygon, tx: f64, ty: f64) -> Polygon {
    Polygon {
        vertices: poly.vertices.iter().map(|p| Point { x: p.x + tx, y: p.y + ty }).collect(),
    }
}

fn ccw(a: &Point, b: &Point, c: &Point) -> f64 {
    (c.y - a.y) * (b.x - a.x) - (b.y - a.y) * (c.x - a.x)
}

fn edges_intersect(p1: &Point, p2: &Point, p3: &Point, p4: &Point) -> bool {
    let cp1 = ccw(p1, p3, p4);
    let cp2 = ccw(p2, p3, p4);
    let cp3 = ccw(p1, p2, p3);
    let cp4 = ccw(p1, p2, p4);
    cp1 * cp2 < 0.0 && cp3 * cp4 < 0.0
}

fn point_in_polygon_fast(pt: &Point, edges: &[Edge]) -> bool {
    let mut c = false;
    for e in edges {
        if ((e.p1.y > pt.y) != (e.p2.y > pt.y)) &&
            (pt.x < (e.p2.x - e.p1.x) * (pt.y - e.p1.y) / (e.p2.y - e.p1.y) + e.p1.x) {
            c = !c;
        }
    }
    c
}

fn polygon_contains(stock_edges: &[Edge], piece: &Polygon) -> bool {
    for pt in &piece.vertices {
        if !point_in_polygon_fast(pt, stock_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    let piece_edges = build_edges(piece);
    for pe in &piece_edges {
        for se in stock_edges {
            if aabb_overlap(&pe.aabb, &se.aabb) {
                if edges_intersect(&pe.p1, &pe.p2, &se.p1, &se.p2) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    for se in stock_edges {
        if point_in_polygon_fast(&se.p1, &piece_edges) {
            return false;
        }
    }
    true
}

struct ShelfStock {
    current_x: f64,
    current_y: f64,
    shelf_height: f64,
}

impl ShelfStock {
    fn new(stock_aabb: &AABB) -> Self {
        ShelfStock {
            current_x: stock_aabb.min_x,
            current_y: stock_aabb.min_y,
            shelf_height: 0.0,
        }
    }
}

fn try_place(
    piece: &Polygon, 
    stock_edges: &[Edge], 
    stock_aabb: &AABB, 
    stock_state: &mut ShelfStock, 
    stock_idx: usize,
    step_x: f64,
    step_y: f64
) -> Option<(usize, f64, f64, f64)> {
    let angles = [0.0, PI / 2.0, PI, 3.0 * PI / 2.0];
    
    let original_cx = stock_state.current_x;
    let original_cy = stock_state.current_y;
    let original_sh = stock_state.shelf_height;
    
    let mut best_placement = None;
    let mut best_waste = f64::MAX;

    for &angle in &angles {
        let rotated_piece = rotate(piece, angle);
        let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&rotated_piece);
        let piece_w = piece_aabb.max_x - piece_aabb.min_x;
        let piece_h = piece_aabb.max_y - piece_aabb.min_y;
        
        let mut cx = original_cx;
        let mut cy = original_cy;
        let mut sh = original_sh;
        
        while cy + piece_h <= stock_aabb.max_y {
            if cx + piece_w <= stock_aabb.max_x {
                let tx = cx - piece_aabb.min_x + 1e-5;
                let ty = cy - piece_aabb.min_y + 1e-5;
                let translated_piece = translate(&rotated_piece, tx, ty);
                
                if polygon_contains(stock_edges, &translated_piece) {
                    let waste = cy * 100000.0 + cx; 
                    if waste < best_waste {
                        best_waste = waste;
                        best_placement = Some((stock_idx, tx, ty, angle, cx, cy, sh, piece_w, piece_h));
                    }
                    break; 
                } else {
                    cx += step_x;
                }
            } else {
                if sh > 0.0 {
                    cy += sh;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                    sh = 0.0;
                } else {
                    cy += step_y;
                    cx = stock_aabb.min_x;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if let Some(p) = best_placement {
        stock_state.current_x = p.4 + p.7 + 1e-5;
        stock_state.shelf_height = p.6.max(p.8 + 1e-5);
        stock_state.current_y = p.5;
        return Some((p.0, p.1, p.2, p.3));
    }
    None
}

fn main() {
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut lines = stdin.lock().lines().filter_map(Result::ok).filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty());
    
    let first_line = lines.next().unwrap();
    let parts: Vec<&str> = first_line.split_whitespace().collect();
    let sv: usize = parts[0].parse().unwrap();
    let np: usize = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
    
    let mut stock_vertices = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..sv {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        stock_vertices.push(Point {
            x: parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
            y: parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
        });
    }
    let stock = Polygon { vertices: stock_vertices };
    
    let mut pieces = Vec::new();
    for _ in 0..np {
        let line = lines.next().unwrap();
        let pv: usize = line.trim().parse().unwrap();
        let mut piece_vertices = Vec::new();
        for _ in 0..pv {
            let p_line = lines.next().unwrap();
            let p_parts: Vec<&str> = p_line.split_whitespace().collect();
            piece_vertices.push(Point {
                x: p_parts[0].parse().unwrap(),
                y: p_parts[1].parse().unwrap(),
            });
        }
        pieces.push(Polygon { vertices: piece_vertices });
    }
    
    let mut pieces_with_idx: Vec<(usize, Polygon)> = pieces.into_iter().enumerate().collect();
    pieces_with_idx.sort_by(|a, b| {
        let a_aabb = get_aabb(&a.1);
        let b_aabb = get_aabb(&b.1);
        let a_max = (a_aabb.max_x - a_aabb.min_x).max(a_aabb.max_y - a_aabb.min_y);
        let b_max = (b_aabb.max_x - b_aabb.min_x).max(b_aabb.max_y - b_aabb.min_y);
        b_max.partial_cmp(&a_max).unwrap()
    });
    
    let stock_aabb = get_aabb(&stock);
    let stock_edges = build_edges(&stock);
    
    let mut step_x = (stock_aabb.max_x - stock_aabb.min_x) / 50.0;
    if step_x <= 1e-5 { step_x = 1.0; }
    let mut step_y = (stock_aabb.max_y - stock_aabb.min_y) / 50.0;
    if step_y <= 1e-5 { step_y = 1.0; }
    
    let mut stocks_state = vec![ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb)];
    let mut results = vec![(0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0); np];
    
    for (orig_idx, piece_poly) in pieces_with_idx {
        let mut placed = false;
        for stock_idx in 0..stocks_state.len() {
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[stock_idx], 
                stock_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
                placed = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if !placed {
            let new_idx = stocks_state.len();
            stocks_state.push(ShelfStock::new(&stock_aabb));
            if let Some((idx, tx, ty, angle)) = try_place(
                &piece_poly, 
                &stock_edges, 
                &stock_aabb, 
                &mut stocks_state[new_idx], 
                new_idx, 
                step_x, 
                step_y
            ) {
                results[orig_idx] = (idx, tx, ty, angle);
            } else {
                let piece_aabb = get_aabb(&piece_poly);
                let cx = (stock_aabb.min_x + stock_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let cy = (stock_aabb.min_y + stock_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                let pcx = (piece_aabb.min_x + piece_aabb.max_x) / 2.0;
                let pcy = (piece_aabb.min_y + piece_aabb.max_y) / 2.0;
                results[orig_idx] = (new_idx, cx - pcx, cy - pcy, 0.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!("{}", stocks_state.len());
    for r in results {
        println!("{} {} {} {}", r.0, r.1, r.2, r.3);
    }
}

Typical Prompt:
You are solving a 3D Bin Packing problem in C#.

You must write a C# solver that can handle ANY problem size from trivial to ludicrous scale:
- **Trivial**: Small containers (5x5x5), simple polyhedra
- **Medium**: Medium containers (10x10x10-20x20x20)
- **Large**: Large containers (50x50x50-100x100x100)
- **Extreme**: Massive containers (200x200x200-500x500x500)

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: V F (vertex/face count of the polyhedron)
Next V lines: x y z (polyhedron vertices)
Next F lines: a b c (polyhedron face indices)
Last line: W H D (container width, height, depth)
Container origin at (0,0,0), extends to (W,H,D).

**Output format (stdout):**
Line 1: count (number of polyhedra packed)
Next count lines: tx ty tz qw qx qy qz
tx,ty,tz: translation
qw,qx,qy,qz: rotation quaternion (w is scalar part)

**Quaternion Rotation Reference:**
- Identity (no rotation): 1 0 0 0
- 90° around Z: 0.707 0 0 0.707
- To rotate a point: p' = q * p * q^(-1)

**Critical Requirements:**
1. **Scalability**: Your algorithm must adapt based on container size and polyhedron complexity
2. **Performance**: Must complete within 5 minutes even for massive containers
3. **Quality**: Maximize packing count while ensuring valid placements

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Globalization;
using System.IO;
using System.Threading.Tasks;

namespace BinPackingSolver
{
    struct Vector3
    {
        public double X, Y, Z;
        public Vector3(double x, double y, double z) { X = x; Y = y; Z = z; }
    }

    struct Quaternion
    {
        public double W, X, Y, Z;
        public Quaternion(double w, double x, double y, double z) { W = w; X = x; Y = y; Z = z; }
        
        public static readonly Quaternion Identity = new Quaternion(1, 0, 0, 0);

        public Vector3 Rotate(Vector3 v)
        {
            double tx = 2 * (Y * v.Z - Z * v.Y);
            double ty = 2 * (Z * v.X - X * v.Z);
            double tz = 2 * (X * v.Y - Y * v.X);

            double rx = v.X + W * tx + (Y * tz - Z * ty);
            double ry = v.Y + W * ty + (Z * tx - X * tz);
            double rz = v.Z + W * tz + (X * ty - Y * tx);

            return new Vector3(rx, ry, rz);
        }

        public static Quaternion FromAxisAngle(Vector3 axis, double angle)
        {
            double halfAngle = angle * 0.5;
            double s = Math.Sin(halfAngle);
            return new Quaternion(Math.Cos(halfAngle), axis.X * s, axis.Y * s, axis.Z * s);
        }

        public static Quaternion Multiply(Quaternion q1, Quaternion q2)
        {
            return new Quaternion(
                q1.W * q2.W - q1.X * q2.X - q1.Y * q2.Y - q1.Z * q2.Z,
                q1.W * q2.X + q1.X * q2.W + q1.Y * q2.Z - q1.Z * q2.Y,
                q1.W * q2.Y - q1.X * q2.Z + q1.Y * q2.W + q1.Z * q2.X,
                q1.W * q2.Z + q1.X * q2.Y - q1.Y * q2.X + q1.Z * q2.W
            );
        }
    }

    class Polyhedron
    {
        public List<Vector3> Vertices;
    }

    class Scanner
    {
        private StreamReader _reader;
        private string[] _tokens = new string[0];
        private int _pos = 0;

        public Scanner(Stream stream)
        {
            _reader = new StreamReader(stream, new System.Text.UTF8Encoding(false), true, 65536);
        }

        public string Next()
        {
            while (_pos >= _tokens.Length)
            {
                string line = _reader.ReadLine();
                if (line == null) return null;
                _tokens = line.Split(new[] { ' ', '\t', '\r', '\n' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
                _pos = 0;
            }
            return _tokens[_pos++];
        }

        public double NextDouble()
        {
            return double.Parse(Next(), CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
        }
        
        public int NextInt()
        {
            return int.Parse(Next(), CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
        }
    }

    class Program
    {
        static void Main()
        {
            var scanner = new Scanner(Console.OpenStandardInput());
            
            string vStr = scanner.Next();
            if (vStr == null) return;
            
            int V = int.Parse(vStr, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
            int F = scanner.NextInt();

            var poly = new Polyhedron { Vertices = new List<Vector3>(V) };
            for (int i = 0; i < V; i++)
            {
                poly.Vertices.Add(new Vector3(
                    scanner.NextDouble(),
                    scanner.NextDouble(),
                    scanner.NextDouble()
                ));
            }

            for (int i = 0; i < F; i++)
            {
                scanner.Next();
                scanner.Next();
                scanner.Next();
            }

            double W = scanner.NextDouble();
            double H = scanner.NextDouble();
            double D = scanner.NextDouble();

            double volume = W * H * D;

            List<Quaternion> rotations;
            if (volume < 50 * 50 * 50)
            {
                rotations = GenerateRotations(10); 
            }
            else if (volume < 150 * 150 * 150)
            {
                rotations = GenerateRotations(30); 
            }
            else
            {
                rotations = GenerateRotations(90); 
            }

            PackAndPrint(poly, W, H, D, rotations);
        }

        static List<Quaternion> GenerateRotations(int stepDegrees)
        {
            var rotations = new List<Quaternion>();
            for (int x = 0; x < 360; x += stepDegrees)
            {
                for (int y = 0; y < 360; y += stepDegrees)
                {
                    for (int z = 0; z < 360; z += stepDegrees)
                    {
                        Quaternion qx = Quaternion.FromAxisAngle(new Vector3(1, 0, 0), x * Math.PI / 180.0);
                        Quaternion qy = Quaternion.FromAxisAngle(new Vector3(0, 1, 0), y * Math.PI / 180.0);
                        Quaternion qz = Quaternion.FromAxisAngle(new Vector3(0, 0, 1), z * Math.PI / 180.0);
                        rotations.Add(Quaternion.Multiply(qx, Quaternion.Multiply(qy, qz)));
                    }
                }
            }
            return rotations;
        }

        static void PackAndPrint(Polyhedron poly, double W, double H, double D, List<Quaternion> rotations)
        {
            long bestCount = -1;
            Quaternion bestRot = Quaternion.Identity;
            double bestBw = 0, bestBh = 0, bestBd = 0;
            double bestMinX = 0, bestMinY = 0, bestMinZ = 0;

            object syncLock = new object();

            Parallel.ForEach(rotations, q =>
            {
                double minX = double.MaxValue, maxX = double.MinValue;
                double minY = double.MaxValue, maxY = double.MinValue;
                double minZ = double.MaxValue, maxZ = double.MinValue;

                foreach (var v in poly.Vertices)
                {
                    Vector3 rv = q.Rotate(v);
                    if (rv.X < minX) minX = rv.X;
                    if (rv.X > maxX) maxX = rv.X;
                    if (rv.Y < minY) minY = rv.Y;
                    if (rv.Y > maxY) maxY = rv.Y;
                    if (rv.Z < minZ) minZ = rv.Z;
                    if (rv.Z > maxZ) maxZ = rv.Z;
                }

                double bw = maxX - minX + 1e-9;
                double bh = maxY - minY + 1e-9;
                double bd = maxZ - minZ + 1e-9;

                if (bw > W || bh > H || bd > D) return;

                long countX = (long)(W / bw);
                long countY = (long)(H / bh);
                long countZ = (long)(D / bd);
                long count = countX * countY * countZ;

                lock (syncLock)
                {
                    if (count > bestCount)
                    {
                        bestCount = count;
                        bestRot = q;
                        bestBw = bw;
                        bestBh = bh;
                        bestBd = bd;
                        bestMinX = minX;
                        bestMinY = minY;
                        bestMinZ = minZ;
                    }
                }
            });

            if (bestCount <= 0)
            {
                Console.WriteLine(0);
                return;
            }

            long cX = (long)(W / bestBw);
            long cY = (long)(H / bestBh);
            long cZ = (long)(D / bestBd);

            using (var stdout = new StreamWriter(Console.OpenStandardOutput(), new System.Text.UTF8Encoding(false), 1048576))
            {
                stdout.WriteLine(bestCount);
                
                string rotStr = $"{bestRot.W.ToString("G17", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)} {bestRot.X.ToString("G17", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)} {bestRot.Y.ToString("G17", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)} {bestRot.Z.ToString("G17", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)}";

                for (long i = 0; i < cX; i++)
                {
                    double tx = i * bestBw - bestMinX;
                    string txStr = tx.ToString("G17", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
                    for (long j = 0; j < cY; j++)
                    {
                        double ty = j * bestBh - bestMinY;
                        string tyStr = ty.ToString("G17", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
                        for (long k = 0; k < cZ; k++)
                        {
                            double tz = k * bestBd - bestMinZ;
                            stdout.WriteLine($"{txStr} {tyStr} {tz.ToString("G17", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)} {rotStr}");
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

Test 13: Longest Common Substring (C++) Score: 0.00 / 12
Typical Prompt:
You are solving the Longest Common Substring problem in C++.

You must write a C++ solver that can handle ANY problem size from trivial to ludicrous scale:
- **Trivial**: 2-3 short strings (10-50 chars each)
- **Medium**: 3-5 medium strings (100-500 chars each)
- **Large**: 5-10 long strings (1000-5000 chars each)
- **Extreme**: 100 very long strings (10MB+ each), massive search space

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: N (number of strings)
Next N lines: one string per line

**Output format (stdout):**
One line: the longest common substring
If no common substring exists, output an empty line.

**Example:**
Input:
3
abcdef
xbcdey
zbcdew

Output:
bcde

**Critical Requirements:**
1. **Scalability**: Your algorithm must adapt based on number and length of strings
2. **Performance**: Must complete within 300 seconds even for very long strings
3. **Correctness**: Must find the actual longest common substring

**Environment:**
Platform: Windows 11 (build 10.0.26200)
Architecture: AMD64
CPU: Intel64 Family 6 Model 158 Stepping 10, GenuineIntel
Core count: 12

Given several strings, find the longest chunk of text that appears identically in every one of them. For example, if the strings are “abcdef” and “xbcdey”, the answer is “bcde”.

Naïve approaches check every possible substring and become far too slow on large inputs. Subpasses increase the string lengths into the millions, so the AI must use efficient data structures or hashing. The baseline uses a simple library call that times out on the bigger cases.

#include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <string>
#include <algorithm>

using namespace std;

// Suffix Automaton Node
struct State {
    int len;
    int link;
    int min_len;
    int head_edge;
    int first_pos;
};

// Edge for Left-Child Right-Sibling representation of transitions
struct Edge {
    uint8_t c;
    int to;
    int next;
};

vector<State> st;
vector<Edge> edges;
int sz, last;

void sam_init(int max_len) {
    // A suffix automaton for a string of length L has at most 2L-1 states and 3L-4 edges.
    st.reserve(max_len * 2 + 10);
    edges.reserve(max_len * 3 + 10);
    st.push_back({0, -1, 0, -1, -1});
    sz = 1;
    last = 0;
}

int get_next(int v, uint8_t c) {
    for (int e = st[v].head_edge; e != -1; e = edges[e].next) {
        if (edges[e].c == c) return edges[e].to;
    }
    return -1;
}

void set_next(int v, uint8_t c, int to) {
    for (int e = st[v].head_edge; e != -1; e = edges[e].next) {
        if (edges[e].c == c) {
            edges[e].to = to;
            return;
        }
    }
    edges.push_back({c, to, st[v].head_edge});
    st[v].head_edge = (int)edges.size() - 1;
}

void sam_extend(uint8_t c) {
    int cur = sz++;
    st.push_back({st[last].len + 1, -1, 0, -1, st[last].len});
    int p = last;
    while (p != -1 && get_next(p, c) == -1) {
        set_next(p, c, cur);
        p = st[p].link;
    }
    if (p == -1) {
        st[cur].link = 0;
    } else {
        int q = get_next(p, c);
        if (st[p].len + 1 == st[q].len) {
            st[cur].link = q;
        } else {
            int clone = sz++;
            st.push_back({st[p].len + 1, st[q].link, 0, -1, st[q].first_pos});
            for (int e = st[q].head_edge; e != -1; e = edges[e].next) {
                set_next(clone, edges[e].c, edges[e].to);
            }
            while (p != -1 && get_next(p, c) == q) {
                set_next(p, c, clone);
                p = st[p].link;
            }
            st[q].link = st[cur].link = clone;
        }
    }
    last = cur;
}

int main() {
    // Optimize I/O operations for reading massive strings rapidly
    ios_base::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(NULL);
    
    int n;
    if (!(cin >> n)) return 0;
    
    string dummy;
    getline(cin, dummy); // Consume the remainder of the first line
    
    vector<string> s;
    s.reserve(n);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) {
        string line;
        if (!getline(cin, line)) break;
        if (!line.empty() && line.back() == '\r') {
            line.pop_back(); // Handle Windows CRLF endings seamlessly
        }
        s.push_back(line);
    }
    
    n = (int)s.size();
    
    if (n == 0) {
        cout << "\n";
        return 0;
    }
    if (n == 1) {
        cout << s[0] << "\n";
        return 0;
    }
    
    // Adaptive Logic:
    // Finding the shortest string and using it as the foundation for the Suffix Automaton.
    // This allows the algorithm to natively adapt to any problem scale (trivial to extreme).
    // The Automaton's memory and state-count is strictly constrained by the smallest string.
    int min_idx = 0;
    for (int i = 1; i < n; ++i) {
        if (s[i].length() < s[min_idx].length()) {
            min_idx = i;
        }
    }
    swap(s[0], s[min_idx]);
    
    sam_init((int)s[0].length());
    for (char c : s[0]) {
        sam_extend((uint8_t)c);
    }
    
    for (int i = 0; i < sz; ++i) {
        st[i].min_len = st[i].len;
    }
    
    // Counting sort of states by length, required for correct suffix link propagation
    vector<int> cnt(s[0].length() + 1, 0);
    for (int i = 0; i < sz; ++i) cnt[st[i].len]++;
    for (int i = 1; i <= (int)s[0].length(); ++i) cnt[i] += cnt[i - 1];
    vector<int> sorted_order(sz);
    for (int i = 0; i < sz; ++i) {
        sorted_order[--cnt[st[i].len]] = i;
    }
    
    // Process all remaining strings through the Automaton
    for (int i = 1; i < n; ++i) {
        vector<int> max_l(sz, 0);
        int p = 0;
        int l = 0;
        for (char ch : s[i]) {
            uint8_t c = (uint8_t)ch;
            while (p != -1 && get_next(p, c) == -1) {
                p = st[p].link;
                l = (p == -1) ? 0 : st[p].len;
            }
            if (p != -1) {
                p = get_next(p, c);
                l++;
            } else {
                p = 0;
                l = 0;
            }
            if (max_l[p] < l) max_l[p] = l;
        }
        
        // Propagate matching lengths backwards through the suffix links
        for (int j = sz - 1; j >= 0; --j) {
            int v = sorted_order[j];
            if (st[v].min_len > max_l[v]) {
                st[v].min_len = max_l[v];
            }
            int link = st[v].link;
            if (link != -1) {
                int val = max_l[v];
                if (val > st[link].len) val = st[link].len;
                if (max_l[link] < val) {
                    max_l[link] = val;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    int best_len = 0;
    int best_state = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < sz; ++i) {
        if (st[i].min_len > best_len) {
            best_len = st[i].min_len;
            best_state = i;
        }
    }
    
    if (best_len == 0) {
        cout << "\n";
    } else {
        int start_pos = st[best_state].first_pos - best_len + 1;
        cout << s[0].substr(start_pos, best_len) << "\n";
    }
    
    return 0;
}

Test 14: Minesweeper Solver (C#) Score: 0.00 / 10
Typical Prompt:
You are writing a Minesweeper solver in C# that must handle ANY board complexity from trivial to ludicrous scale.

- **Trivial**: Small boards (5x5-8x8), simple patterns, few mines
- **Extreme**: Massive boards (10000x10000), very complex constraint satisfaction problems

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: H W (height and width)
Next H lines: the board row strings (each W characters)

**Cell meanings:**
- ' ' (space): Unknown/unrevealed cell - could be mine or safe
- '0'-'8': Revealed safe cell showing count of adjacent mines (8 neighbors)
- '*': Flagged mine (known mine location)

**Output format (stdout):**
Line 1: N (number of safe cells found)
Next N lines: x y (column row, 0-indexed)
Only output cells that are currently unknown (' ') and provably safe.
Do NOT guess - only return cells you can prove are safe.

**Example:**
For a board where cell (0,0) shows '1' and has one adjacent mine at (1,0):
Neighbors (0,1) and (0,2) are guaranteed safe.

**Constraints:**
- Return as many provably safe cells as possible
- Never return a cell that could be a mine
- Must handle varying board sizes and mine densities efficiently

**Environment:**
Platform: Windows 11 (build 10.0.26200)
Architecture: AMD64
CPU: Intel64 Family 6 Model 158 Stepping 10, GenuineIntel
Core count: 12
Memory: 31.93 GB

SIMD detail: AVX=yes, AVX-512F=no, AVX2=yes, SSE=yes, SSE2=yes, SSE3=yes, SSE4.1=yes, SSE4.2=yes, SSSE3=yes

C# (.NET SDK 10.0.201; SDKs 10.0.201) | csc 5.3.0-2.26153.122 (4d3023de605a78ba3e59e50c657eed70f125c68a) | max LangVersion 14
