Given a partially-revealed Minesweeper board, deduce which hidden cells are safe to click and which contain mines. Each visible number tells you exactly how many of its neighbours are mined — the AI must combine these clues to make guaranteed-safe moves without guessing.

Larger boards and denser mine layouts make the logic harder. The problem is NP-complete in general, but clever constraint reasoning can solve most practical boards. The baseline uses only the simplest single-cell deduction rules.

Minesweeper Solver - 8x8 board, 10 mines

View Code (18722 chars)
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;

class MinesweeperSolver
{
    static int H, W;
    static char[,] grid;
    static int[] dr = { -1, -1, -1, 0, 0, 1, 1, 1 };
    static int[] dc = { -1, 0, 1, -1, 1, -1, 0, 1 };
    static HashSet<int> activeEqs = new HashSet<int>();

    class Eq {
        public int R, C;
        public List<int> Vars;
        public int Target;
    }

    static void Main()
    {
        string header = Console.ReadLine();
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(header)) return;
        string[] hw = header.Split(new char[] { ' ', '\t' }, StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
        if (hw.Length < 2) return;
        H = int.Parse(hw[0]);
        W = int.Parse(hw[1]);

        grid = new char[H, W];
        for (int i = 0; i < H; i++)
        {
            string line = Console.ReadLine();
            for (int j = 0; j < W; j++)
            {
                grid[i, j] = line[j];
            }
        }

        for (int r = 0; r < H; r++)
        {
            for (int c = 0; c < W; c++)
            {
                if (grid[r, c] >= '1' && grid[r, c] <= '8')
                {
                    int unknowns = 0;
                    for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
                    {
                        int nr = r + dr[i];
                        int nc = c + dc[i];
                        if (nr >= 0 && nr < H && nc >= 0 && nc < W && grid[nr, nc] == ' ') unknowns++;
                    }
                    if (unknowns > 0) activeEqs.Add(r * W + c);
                }
            }
        }

        Queue<int> safes = new Queue<int>();
        Queue<int> mines = new Queue<int>();

        List<int> initialActive = activeEqs.ToList();
        foreach (var id in initialActive)
        {
            ReEvaluate(id / W, id % W, safes, mines);
        }

        bool changed = true;
        while (changed)
        {
            changed = false;

            if (safes.Count > 0 || mines.Count > 0)
            {
                Propagate(safes, mines);
                changed = true;
                continue;
            }

            if (ApplySubsetRules(safes, mines))
            {
                changed = true;
                continue;
            }

            if (ApplyBacktracking(safes, mines))
            {
                changed = true;
                continue;
            }
        }

        List<int> resultSafes = new List<int>();
        for (int r = 0; r < H; r++)
        {
            for (int c = 0; c < W; c++)
            {
                if (grid[r, c] == 'S')
                {
                    resultSafes.Add(r * W + c);
                }
            }
        }

        Console.WriteLine(resultSafes.Count);
        foreach (var id in resultSafes)
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"{id % W} {id / W}");
        }
    }

    static void ReEvaluate(int r, int c, Queue<int> safes, Queue<int> mines)
    {
        int target = grid[r, c] - '0';
        int unknowns = 0;
        int knownMines = 0;

        for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
        {
            int nr = r + dr[i];
            int nc = c + dc[i];
            if (nr >= 0 && nr < H && nc >= 0 && nc < W)
            {
                char v = grid[nr, nc];
                if (v == ' ') unknowns++;
                else if (v == '*' || v == 'M') knownMines++;
            }
        }

        int id = r * W + c;
        if (unknowns == 0)
        {
            activeEqs.Remove(id);
            return;
        }
        else
        {
            activeEqs.Add(id);
        }

        int rem = target - knownMines;
        if (rem == 0 && unknowns > 0)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
            {
                int nr = r + dr[i];
                int nc = c + dc[i];
                if (nr >= 0 && nr < H && nc >= 0 && nc < W)
                {
                    if (grid[nr, nc] == ' ')
                    {
                        grid[nr, nc] = 'S';
                        safes.Enqueue(nr * W + nc);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else if (rem == unknowns && unknowns > 0)
        {
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
            {
                int nr = r + dr[i];
                int nc = c + dc[i];
                if (nr >= 0 && nr < H && nc >= 0 && nc < W)
                {
                    if (grid[nr, nc] == ' ')
                    {
                        grid[nr, nc] = 'M';
                        mines.Enqueue(nr * W + nc);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    static void Propagate(Queue<int> safes, Queue<int> mines)
    {
        while (safes.Count > 0 || mines.Count > 0)
        {
            if (safes.Count > 0)
            {
                int id = safes.Dequeue();
                int r = id / W;
                int c = id % W;
                for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
                {
                    int nr = r + dr[i];
                    int nc = c + dc[i];
                    if (nr >= 0 && nr < H && nc >= 0 && nc < W)
                    {
                        if (grid[nr, nc] >= '1' && grid[nr, nc] <= '8')
                        {
                            ReEvaluate(nr, nc, safes, mines);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            if (mines.Count > 0)
            {
                int id = mines.Dequeue();
                int r = id / W;
                int c = id % W;
                for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
                {
                    int nr = r + dr[i];
                    int nc = c + dc[i];
                    if (nr >= 0 && nr < H && nc >= 0 && nc < W)
                    {
                        if (grid[nr, nc] >= '1' && grid[nr, nc] <= '8')
                        {
                            ReEvaluate(nr, nc, safes, mines);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    static List<Eq> BuildEquations()
    {
        List<Eq> eqs = new List<Eq>();
        List<int> toRemove = new List<int>();

        foreach (var id in activeEqs)
        {
            int r = id / W;
            int c = id % W;
            int target = grid[r, c] - '0';
            List<int> vars = new List<int>();
            int knownMines = 0;

            for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
            {
                int nr = r + dr[i];
                int nc = c + dc[i];
                if (nr >= 0 && nr < H && nc >= 0 && nc < W)
                {
                    char v = grid[nr, nc];
                    if (v == ' ') vars.Add(nr * W + nc);
                    else if (v == '*' || v == 'M') knownMines++;
                }
            }

            if (vars.Count > 0)
            {
                eqs.Add(new Eq
                {
                    R = r,
                    C = c,
                    Vars = vars,
                    Target = target - knownMines
                });
            }
            else
            {
                toRemove.Add(id);
            }
        }

        foreach (var id in toRemove) activeEqs.Remove(id);
        return eqs;
    }

    static bool ApplySubsetRules(Queue<int> safes, Queue<int> mines)
    {
        var eqs = BuildEquations();
        if (eqs.Count == 0) return false;

        Dictionary<int, List<Eq>> varToEqs = new Dictionary<int, List<Eq>>();
        foreach (var eq in eqs)
        {
            foreach (var v in eq.Vars)
            {
                if (!varToEqs.ContainsKey(v)) varToEqs[v] = new List<Eq>();
                varToEqs[v].Add(eq);
            }
        }

        bool madeProgress = false;
        HashSet<long> checkedPairs = new HashSet<long>();

        foreach (var kvp in varToEqs)
        {
            var list = kvp.Value;
            for (int i = 0; i < list.Count; i++)
            {
                for (int j = i + 1; j < list.Count; j++)
                {
                    var e1 = list[i];
                    var e2 = list[j];

                    long id1 = (long)e1.R * W + e1.C;
                    long id2 = (long)e2.R * W + e2.C;
                    long pairId = id1 < id2 ? (id1 << 32) | id2 : (id2 << 32) | id1;

                    if (!checkedPairs.Add(pairId)) continue;

                    var eqA = e1;
                    var eqB = e2;
                    if (eqA.Vars.Count > eqB.Vars.Count)
                    {
                        eqA = e2; eqB = e1;
                    }
                    else if (eqA.Vars.Count == eqB.Vars.Count)
                    {
                        continue;
                    }

                    bool isSubset = true;
                    foreach (var v in eqA.Vars)
                    {
                        if (!eqB.Vars.Contains(v))
                        {
                            isSubset = false; break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (isSubset)
                    {
                        int newTarget = eqB.Target - eqA.Target;
                        int newCount = eqB.Vars.Count - eqA.Vars.Count;

                        if (newTarget == 0)
                        {
                            foreach (var v in eqB.Vars)
                            {
                                if (!eqA.Vars.Contains(v))
                                {
                                    if (grid[v / W, v % W] == ' ')
                                    {
                                        grid[v / W, v % W] = 'S';
                                        safes.Enqueue(v);
                                        madeProgress = true;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        else if (newTarget == newCount)
                        {
                            foreach (var v in eqB.Vars)
                            {
                                if (!eqA.Vars.Contains(v))
                                {
                                    if (grid[v / W, v % W] == ' ')
                                    {
                                        grid[v / W, v % W] = 'M';
                                        mines.Enqueue(v);
                                        madeProgress = true;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        if (madeProgress) return true;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    static bool ApplyBacktracking(Queue<int> safes, Queue<int> mines)
    {
        var eqs = BuildEquations();
        if (eqs.Count == 0) return false;

        HashSet<int> allVars = new HashSet<int>();
        foreach (var eq in eqs) foreach (var v in eq.Vars) allVars.Add(v);

        Dictionary<int, List<Eq>> varToEqs = new Dictionary<int, List<Eq>>();
        foreach (var v in allVars) varToEqs[v] = new List<Eq>();
        foreach (var eq in eqs)
        {
            foreach (var v in eq.Vars)
            {
                varToEqs[v].Add(eq);
            }
        }

        HashSet<int> visitedVars = new HashSet<int>();
        bool madeProgress = false;

        foreach (var startVar in allVars)
        {
            if (visitedVars.Contains(startVar)) continue;

            List<int> compVars = new List<int>();
            HashSet<Eq> compEqs = new HashSet<Eq>();

            Queue<int> q = new Queue<int>();
            q.Enqueue(startVar);
            visitedVars.Add(startVar);

            while (q.Count > 0)
            {
                int curr = q.Dequeue();
                compVars.Add(curr);

                foreach (var eq in varToEqs[curr])
                {
                    if (compEqs.Add(eq))
                    {
                        foreach (var nxt in eq.Vars)
                        {
                            if (visitedVars.Add(nxt))
                            {
                                q.Enqueue(nxt);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            int N = compVars.Count;
            int M = compEqs.Count;

            Dictionary<int, int> varToIndex = new Dictionary<int, int>();
            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) varToIndex[compVars[i]] = i;

            var localEqs = compEqs.ToList();

            int[] eqTarget = new int[M];
            int[] eqAssignedSum = new int[M];
            int[] eqRemainingVars = new int[M];
            
            List<int>[] varToEqIndicesList = new List<int>[N];
            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) varToEqIndicesList[i] = new List<int>();

            for (int i = 0; i < M; i++)
            {
                eqTarget[i] = localEqs[i].Target;
                eqRemainingVars[i] = localEqs[i].Vars.Count;
                foreach (var v in localEqs[i].Vars)
                {
                    varToEqIndicesList[varToIndex[v]].Add(i);
                }
            }

            int[][] varToEqIndices = new int[N][];
            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) varToEqIndices[i] = varToEqIndicesList[i].ToArray();

            List<int> orderedVars = new List<int>();
            bool[] added = new bool[N];
            List<int>[] varAdj = new List<int>[N];
            for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) varAdj[i] = new List<int>();

            for (int i = 0; i < M; i++)
            {
                var vars = localEqs[i].Vars;
                for (int u = 0; u < vars.Count; u++)
                {
                    for (int v = u + 1; v < vars.Count; v++)
                    {
                        int id1 = varToIndex[vars[u]];
                        int id2 = varToIndex[vars[v]];
                        varAdj[id1].Add(id2);
                        varAdj[id2].Add(id1);
                    }
                }
            }

            Queue<int> orderQ = new Queue<int>();
            orderQ.Enqueue(0);
            added[0] = true;

            while (orderedVars.Count < N)
            {
                if (orderQ.Count == 0)
                {
                    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
                    {
                        if (!added[i])
                        {
                            orderQ.Enqueue(i);
                            added[i] = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                int curr = orderQ.Dequeue();
                orderedVars.Add(curr);
                foreach (var nxt in varAdj[curr])
                {
                    if (!added[nxt])
                    {
                        added[nxt] = true;
                        orderQ.Enqueue(nxt);
                    }
                }
            }

            int[] currentAssignment = new int[N];
            int[] validMineCounts = new int[N];
            int validStates = 0;
            bool limitExceeded = false;

            void SolveCSP(int depth)
            {
                if (limitExceeded) return;

                if (depth == N)
                {
                    for (int i = 0; i < M; i++)
                    {
                        if (eqAssignedSum[i] != eqTarget[i]) return;
                    }
                    validStates++;
                    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
                    {
                        if (currentAssignment[i] == 1) validMineCounts[i]++;
                    }
                    if (validStates > 50000)
                    {
                        limitExceeded = true;
                    }
                    return;
                }

                int varIndex = orderedVars[depth];
                var eqIndices = varToEqIndices[varIndex];

                bool canBe0 = true;
                for (int i = 0; i < eqIndices.Length; i++)
                {
                    int eqIdx = eqIndices[i];
                    if (eqAssignedSum[eqIdx] + eqRemainingVars[eqIdx] - 1 < eqTarget[eqIdx])
                    {
                        canBe0 = false; break;
                    }
                }

                if (canBe0)
                {
                    currentAssignment[varIndex] = 0;
                    for (int i = 0; i < eqIndices.Length; i++)
                    {
                        eqRemainingVars[eqIndices[i]]--;
                    }

                    SolveCSP(depth + 1);

                    for (int i = 0; i < eqIndices.Length; i++)
                    {
                        eqRemainingVars[eqIndices[i]]++;
                    }
                }

                bool canBe1 = true;
                for (int i = 0; i < eqIndices.Length; i++)
                {
                    int eqIdx = eqIndices[i];
                    if (eqAssignedSum[eqIdx] + 1 > eqTarget[eqIdx])
                    {
                        canBe1 = false; break;
                    }
                }

                if (canBe1)
                {
                    currentAssignment[varIndex] = 1;
                    for (int i = 0; i < eqIndices.Length; i++)
                    {
                        eqRemainingVars[eqIndices[i]]--;
                        eqAssignedSum[eqIndices[i]]++;
                    }

                    SolveCSP(depth + 1);

                    for (int i = 0; i < eqIndices.Length; i++)
                    {
                        eqRemainingVars[eqIndices[i]]++;
                        eqAssignedSum[eqIndices[i]]--;
                    }
                }
            }

            SolveCSP(0);

            if (!limitExceeded && validStates > 0)
            {
                for (int i = 0; i < N; i++)
                {
                    if (validMineCounts[i] == 0)
                    {
                        int v = compVars[i];
                        if (grid[v / W, v % W] == ' ')
                        {
                            grid[v / W, v % W] = 'S';
                            safes.Enqueue(v);
                            madeProgress = true;
                        }
                    }
                    else if (validMineCounts[i] == validStates)
                    {
                        int v = compVars[i];
                        if (grid[v / W, v % W] == ' ')
                        {
                            grid[v / W, v % W] = 'M';
                            mines.Enqueue(v);
                            madeProgress = true;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (madeProgress) return true;
        }

        return madeProgress;
    }
}

Test 15: Tetrahedron Shadow Covering (Rust) Score: 11.00 / 11
Typical Prompt:
You are solving a Shadow Covering problem with tetrahedrons in Rust.

**The Challenge:**
Your program will be tested with polygons ranging from simple shapes to very complex geometries.
The same program must work efficiently across ALL scales.

**Input format (stdin):**
Line 1: NV (number of polygon vertices)
Next NV lines: x y (polygon vertices on z=0 plane)
Last line: sx sy sz (sun direction vector, points from sun toward ground)

**Output format (stdout):**
Line 1: count (number of tetrahedrons)
Next count lines: px py pz qw qx qy qz scale
px,py,pz: center position
qw,qx,qy,qz: rotation quaternion (w is scalar)
scale: uniform scale factor

**Standard Tetrahedron Reference:**
Vertices (before transform):
[1.0, 0.0, -0.707]
[-1.0, 0.0, -0.707]
[0.0, 1.0, 0.707]
[0.0, -1.0, 0.707]

**Constraints:**
- Combined shadows must completely cover target polygon
- Tetrahedrons must not intersect each other in 3D
- Maximum scale factor per tetrahedron: 10.0
- Minimize number of tetrahedrons

**Environment:**
Platform: Windows 11 (build 10.0.26200)
Architecture: AMD64
CPU: Intel64 Family 6 Model 158 Stepping 10, GenuineIntel
Core count: 12
Memory: 31.93 GB
SIMD: AVX, AVX2, SSE, SSE2, SSE3, SSE4.1, SSE4.2, SSSE3
SIMD detail: AVX=yes, AVX-512F=no, AVX2=yes, SSE=yes, SSE2=yes, SSE3=yes, SSE4.1=yes, SSE4.2=yes, SSSE3=yes

**Rust Compiler:**
rustc 1.92.0 (ded5c06cf 2025-12-08) | edition=2024 | host: x86_64-pc-windows-msvc

Be aware that default warnings are enabled and will cause a compilation failure,
so ensure that you write warning-free code.

Write complete, compilable Rust code with a main() function.
Include adaptive logic that chooses different strategies based on problem scale.
 Prompt Changes:
Prompt parameters change between subpasses (increasing difficulty)

Place 3D tetrahedra (triangular pyramids) above a flat surface so that their shadows, cast by a directional light, completely cover a given 2D target shape. Use as few tetrahedra as possible while covering every part of the target.

The AI must reason about 3D-to-2D projection, rotation, and coverage geometry. Subpasses use more complex target shapes and trickier light angles. The baseline uses a simple grid of tetrahedra above the target.

 1.0000
[3x3 square, sun straight down] 100% coverage with 1 tetrahedrons, Time: 0.1s

Shadow Covering - 3x3 square, sun straight down

use std::io::{self, Read};
use std::collections::HashSet;

fn main() {
    let mut input = String::new();
    io::stdin().read_to_string(&mut input).unwrap();
    let mut tokens = input.split_whitespace();

    let nv: usize = match tokens.next() {
        Some(s) => s.parse().unwrap(),
        None => return,
    };

    let mut polygon = Vec::with_capacity(nv);
    for _ in 0..nv {
        let x: f64 = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
        let y: f64 = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
        polygon.push((x, y));
    }

    let sx: f64 = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
    let sy: f64 = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
    let sz: f64 = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();

    let s_len = (sx * sx + sy * sy + sz * sz).sqrt();
    let s_norm = (sx / s_len, sy / s_len, sz / s_len);

    let z_col = s_norm;
    let mut a = (0.0, 1.0, 0.0);
    if z_col.1.abs() > 0.99 {
        a = (1.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    }
    
    let mut x_col = (
        a.1 * z_col.2 - a.2 * z_col.1,
        a.2 * z_col.0 - a.0 * z_col.2,
        a.0 * z_col.1 - a.1 * z_col.0,
    );
    let x_len = (x_col.0 * x_col.0 + x_col.1 * x_col.1 + x_col.2 * x_col.2).sqrt();
    x_col = (x_col.0 / x_len, x_col.1 / x_len, x_col.2 / x_len);

    let y_col = (
        z_col.1 * x_col.2 - z_col.2 * x_col.1,
        z_col.2 * x_col.0 - z_col.0 * x_col.2,
        z_col.0 * x_col.1 - z_col.1 * x_col.0,
    );

    let r00 = x_col.0; let r01 = y_col.0; let r02 = z_col.0;
    let r10 = x_col.1; let r11 = y_col.1; let r12 = z_col.1;
    let r20 = x_col.2; let r21 = y_col.2; let r22 = z_col.2;

    let trace = r00 + r11 + r22;
    let (mut qw, mut qx, mut qy, mut qz);
    if trace > 0.0 {
        let s = (trace + 1.0).sqrt() * 2.0;
        qw = 0.25 * s;
        qx = (r21 - r12) / s;
        qy = (r02 - r20) / s;
        qz = (r10 - r01) / s;
    } else if r00 > r11 && r00 > r22 {
        let s = (1.0 + r00 - r11 - r22).sqrt() * 2.0;
        qw = (r21 - r12) / s;
        qx = 0.25 * s;
        qy = (r01 + r10) / s;
        qz = (r02 + r20) / s;
    } else if r11 > r22 {
        let s = (1.0 + r11 - r00 - r22).sqrt() * 2.0;
        qw = (r02 - r20) / s;
        qx = (r01 + r10) / s;
        qy = 0.25 * s;
        qz = (r12 + r21) / s;
    } else {
        let s = (1.0 + r22 - r00 - r11).sqrt() * 2.0;
        qw = (r10 - r01) / s;
        qx = (r02 + r20) / s;
        qy = (r12 + r21) / s;
        qz = 0.25 * s;
    }

    let q_len = (qw*qw + qx*qx + qy*qy + qz*qz).sqrt();
    qw /= q_len; qx /= q_len; qy /= q_len; qz /= q_len;

    let proj = |v: (f64, f64, f64)| -> (f64, f64) {
        let t = v.2 / s_norm.2;
        (v.0 - s_norm.0 * t, v.1 - s_norm.1 * t)
    };

    let p_x_col = proj(x_col);
    let p_y_col = proj(y_col);

    let tet_scale = 10.0;
    
    let mut min_x = f64::INFINITY;
    let mut max_x = f64::NEG_INFINITY;
    let mut min_y = f64::INFINITY;
    let mut max_y = f64::NEG_INFINITY;
    for p in &polygon {
        min_x = min_x.min(p.0);
        max_x = max_x.max(p.0);
        min_y = min_y.min(p.1);
        max_y = max_y.max(p.1);
    }
    
    let offset_x = (min_x + max_x) / 2.0;
    let offset_y = (min_y + max_y) / 2.0;
    
    // ADAPTIVE STRATEGY:
    // If the polygon is small, the grid centers perfectly on the polygon,
    // requiring only a single large tetrahedron that natively encompasses it.
    // For large polygons, we shrink grid_scale slightly (9.9) for 1% overlap,
    // and rely on the scanline algorithm to trace the huge polygon.
    let bbox_width = max_x - min_x;
    let bbox_height = max_y - min_y;
    let is_small = bbox_width < 10.0 && bbox_height < 10.0;
    
    let grid_scale = if is_small { 10.0 } else { 9.9 };

    let v1 = (grid_scale * (p_x_col.0 - p_y_col.0), grid_scale * (p_x_col.1 - p_y_col.1));
    let v2 = (grid_scale * (p_x_col.0 + p_y_col.0), grid_scale * (p_x_col.1 + p_y_col.1));

    let det = v1.0 * v2.1 - v1.1 * v2.0;

    let map_to_nm = |x: f64, y: f64| -> (f64, f64) {
        let dx = x - offset_x;
        let dy = y - offset_y;
        let n = (v2.1 * dx - v2.0 * dy) / det;
        let m = (-v1.1 * dx + v1.0 * dy) / det;
        (n, m)
    };

    let mut mapped_poly = Vec::with_capacity(nv);
    for p in &polygon {
        mapped_poly.push(map_to_nm(p.0, p.1));
    }

    let mut selected_cells = HashSet::new();
    let r = (tet_scale / grid_scale) * 0.5;

    // 1. Edge intersection
    for i in 0..nv {
        let p1 = mapped_poly[i];
        let p2 = mapped_poly[(i + 1) % nv];
        
        let min_n = (p1.0.min(p2.0) - r).floor() as i64;
        let max_n = (p1.0.max(p2.0) + r).ceil() as i64;
        let min_m = (p1.1.min(p2.1) - r).floor() as i64;
        let max_m = (p1.1.max(p2.1) + r).ceil() as i64;

        for n in min_n..=max_n {
            for m in min_m..=max_m {
                if segment_intersects_square(p1, p2, n, m, r) {
                    selected_cells.insert((n, m));
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // 2. Interior fill (scanline)
    let min_m_poly = mapped_poly.iter().map(|p| p.1).fold(f64::INFINITY, |a, b| a.min(b)).floor() as i64;
    let max_m_poly = mapped_poly.iter().map(|p| p.1).fold(f64::NEG_INFINITY, |a, b| a.max(b)).ceil() as i64;

    for m in min_m_poly..=max_m_poly {
        let mut x_ints = Vec::new();
        for i in 0..nv {
            let p1 = mapped_poly[i];
            let p2 = mapped_poly[(i + 1) % nv];
            let y = m as f64;
            
            if (p1.1 < y && p2.1 >= y) || (p2.1 < y && p1.1 >= y) {
                let x = p1.0 + (y - p1.1) * (p2.0 - p1.0) / (p2.1 - p1.1);
                x_ints.push(x);
            }
        }
        
        x_ints.sort_by(|a, b| a.partial_cmp(b).unwrap());
        
        for i in (0..x_ints.len()).step_by(2) {
            if i + 1 < x_ints.len() {
                let start_n = x_ints[i].ceil() as i64;
                let end_n = x_ints[i+1].floor() as i64;
                for n in start_n..=end_n {
                    selected_cells.insert((n, m));
                }
            }
        }
    }

    println!("{}", selected_cells.len());
    let mut i = 0;
    for (n, m) in selected_cells {
        let shadow_x = offset_x + n as f64 * v1.0 + m as f64 * v2.0;
        let shadow_y = offset_y + n as f64 * v1.1 + m as f64 * v2.1;
        
        // Use an extreme Z separation along the sun's rays to strictly avoid 3D intersection
        let p_z = 1000.0 + (i as f64) * 100.0;
        let p_x = shadow_x + (p_z / s_norm.2) * s_norm.0;
        let p_y = shadow_y + (p_z / s_norm.2) * s_norm.1;

        println!("{:.6} {:.6} {:.6} {:.6} {:.6} {:.6} {:.6} {:.6}", 
                 p_x, p_y, p_z, qw, qx, qy, qz, tet_scale);
        i += 1;
    }
}

fn segment_intersects_square(p1: (f64, f64), p2: (f64, f64), n: i64, m: i64, r: f64) -> bool {
    let x_min = n as f64 - r;
    let x_max = n as f64 + r;
    let y_min = m as f64 - r;
    let y_max = m as f64 + r;

    if p1.0 >= x_min && p1.0 <= x_max && p1.1 >= y_min && p1.1 <= y_max { return true; }
    if p2.0 >= x_min && p2.0 <= x_max && p2.1 >= y_min && p2.1 <= y_max { return true; }

    if p1.0.min(p2.0) > x_max || p1.0.max(p2.0) < x_min { return false; }
    if p1.1.min(p2.1) > y_max || p1.1.max(p2.1) < y_min { return false; }

    let edges = [
        ((x_min, y_min), (x_max, y_min)),
        ((x_max, y_min), (x_max, y_max)),
        ((x_max, y_max), (x_min, y_max)),
        ((x_min, y_max), (x_min, y_min)),
    ];

    for e in &edges {
        if segments_intersect(p1, p2, e.0, e.1) {
            return true;
        }
    }
    false
}

fn segments_intersect(p1: (f64, f64), p2: (f64, f64), p3: (f64, f64), p4: (f64, f64)) -> bool {
    let cross = |a: (f64, f64), b: (f64, f64), c: (f64, f64)| {
        (b.0 - a.0) * (c.1 - a.1) - (b.1 - a.1) * (c.0 - a.0)
    };
    let d1 = cross(p3, p4, p1);
    let d2 = cross(p3, p4, p2);
    let d3 = cross(p1, p2, p3);
    let d4 = cross(p1, p2, p4);

    if ((d1 > 0.0 && d2 < 0.0) || (d1 < 0.0 && d2 > 0.0)) &&
       ((d3 > 0.0 && d4 < 0.0) || (d3 < 0.0 && d4 > 0.0)) {
        return true;
    }
    
    if d1 == 0.0 && on_segment(p3, p4, p1) { return true; }
    if d2 == 0.0 && on_segment(p3, p4, p2) { return true; }
    if d3 == 0.0 && on_segment(p1, p2, p3) { return true; }
    if d4 == 0.0 && on_segment(p1, p2, p4) { return true; }

    false
}

fn on_segment(p1: (f64, f64), p2: (f64, f64), p: (f64, f64)) -> bool {
    p.0 >= p1.0.min(p2.0) && p.0 <= p1.0.max(p2.0) &&
    p.1 >= p1.1.min(p2.1) && p.1 <= p1.1.max(p2.1)
}
